   "cell_type": "markdown",

   "source": [
    "# Tutorial\n",
    "\n",
    "We will do the assembly and merging using the example data in the tests/data directory in the following order:\n",
    "\n",
    "1. Preparing sample info spreadsheet\n",
    "2. Preparing inputs\n",
    "3. Assembling individual samples\n",
    "4. Evalulation of individual assemblies\n",
    "5. Preparing for merge\n",
    "6. Merging\n",
    "7. Evaluation of the merged assembly\n",
    "8. Annotating merged assembly\n",
    "\n",
    "The example data is the chromosome 1 portion of the RNASeq data from the neurons in superior central nucleus raphe, medial part (CSm) and dosal nucleus raphe (DR) in Fev-Cre mouse line which labels serotoninergic neurons.  (Fev-Cre is also called ePet-Cre.) \n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [

    "## Sample Info\n",
    "\n",
    "For this tutorial, we will use the Excel file **sampleinfo.xlsx** in the tests/data directory. Following fields are required:\n",
    "\n",
    "- **name**: unique sample name\n",
    "- **mapbed**: name (or path) of BED file containing mapped reads\n",
    "- **sjtab**: name (or path) of STAR SJ.out.tab output file\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 2,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [

      "1  Fev_CSm_m70_1624.chr1  Fev_CSm_m70_1624_star.chr1.bed.gz   \n",
      "2   Fev_DR_m71_1625.chr1   Fev_DR_m71_1625_star.chr1.bed.gz   \n",
      "3  Fev_CSm_m71_1626.chr1  Fev_CSm_m71_1626_star.chr1.bed.gz   \n",
      "\n",
      "                              sjtab  \n",
      "0   Fev_DR_m70_1623.chr1.SJ.out.tab  \n",

     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "import pandas as PD\n",
    "\n",
    "si = PD.read_excel('../tests/data/sampleinfo.xlsx')\n",
    "print(si[['name','mapbed','sjtab']])"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "The read mapping output from STAR is a BAM file. We convert the BAM file to BED file. You can do this using **bedtools bamtobed** command, or using the wrapper [jgem.bedtools.bam2bed](modules.html#jgem.bedtools.bam2bed):\n",
    "\n",
    "```python\n",
    "from jgem import bedtools as BT\n",
    "BT.bam2bed(bam_path,bed_path)\n",
    "```\n",
    "\n",
    "STAR also creates a file named SJ.out.tab which contains junction information. "
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "First, we'll create columns containing actual paths of these files in the sampleinfo dataframe."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 3,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "                    name                                           bed_path  \\\n",
      "0   Fev_DR_m70_1623.chr1  ../tests/data/BED/Fev_DR_m70_1623_star.chr1.be...   \n",
      "1  Fev_CSm_m70_1624.chr1  ../tests/data/BED/Fev_CSm_m70_1624_star.chr1.b...   \n",
      "2   Fev_DR_m71_1625.chr1  ../tests/data/BED/Fev_DR_m71_1625_star.chr1.be...   \n",
      "3  Fev_CSm_m71_1626.chr1  ../tests/data/BED/Fev_CSm_m71_1626_star.chr1.b...   \n",
      "\n",
      "                                          sjtab_path  \n",
      "0   ../tests/data/SJ/Fev_DR_m70_1623.chr1.SJ.out.tab  \n",
      "1  ../tests/data/SJ/Fev_CSm_m70_1624.chr1.SJ.out.tab  \n",
      "2   ../tests/data/SJ/Fev_DR_m71_1625.chr1.SJ.out.tab  \n",
      "3  ../tests/data/SJ/Fev_CSm_m71_1626.chr1.SJ.out.tab  \n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "import os\n",
    "\n",
    "BASEDIR = '../tests/data'\n",
    "si['bed_path'] = [os.path.join(BASEDIR, \"BED\", x) for x in si['mapbed']]\n",
    "si['sjtab_path'] =  [os.path.join(BASEDIR, \"SJ\", x) for x in si['sjtab']]\n",
    "\n",
    "print(si[['name','bed_path','sjtab_path']])"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## Preparing Inputs to the assembler\n",
    "\n",
    "We need a BIGWIG file containing normalized coverages and an appropriately formatted BED file containing junction information for the inputs to the assembler.\n",
    "\n",
    "To normalize coverage, we use average coverage which is the number of the total mapped base pairs divided by the number of covered base pairs. This can be calculated using  [jgem.bedtools.get_total_bp_bedfile](modules.html#jgem.bedtools.get_total_bp_bedfile):"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 4,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "                    name      totbp     covbp       acov\n",
      "0   Fev_DR_m70_1623.chr1  145699916   9142973  15.935726\n",
      "1  Fev_CSm_m70_1624.chr1  158992441  11276760  14.099124\n",
      "2   Fev_DR_m71_1625.chr1  161359243  13946848  11.569585\n",
      "3  Fev_CSm_m71_1626.chr1  161885717  11661445  13.882132\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "# calculate total bp and covered bp, takes ~1min\n",
    "from jgem import bedtools as BT\n",
    "tot_cov = [BT.get_total_bp_bedfile(x) for x in si['bed_path']]\n",
    "si['totbp'] = [x[0] for x in tot_cov]\n",
    "si['covbp'] = [x[1] for x in tot_cov]\n",
    "si['acov'] = si['totbp']/si['covbp']\n",
    "print(si[['name','totbp','covbp','acov']])"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "Now normalized BIGWIG coverage files can be generated using [jgem.bedtools.bed2bw](modules.html#jgem.bedtools.bed2bw) function:"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 5,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": true
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# first prepare destination\n",
    "si['bw_path'] = [os.path.join(BASEDIR, \"bigwig/{0}.bw\".format(x)) for x in si['name']]\n",
    "# then make coverages BIGWIG from BED (~ 2 min)\n",
    "from jgem import utils as UT\n",
    "chromsizes = UT.chromsizes('mm10') # a file containing chromosome names and sizes\n",
    "for bedfile, bwfile, acov in si[['bed_path','bw_path','acov']].values:\n",
    "    scale = 1./acov\n",
    "    BT.bed2bw(bedfile, chromsizes, bwfile, scale)"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 6,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "../tests/data/bigwig/Fev_CSm_m70_1624.chr1.bw\r\n",
      "../tests/data/bigwig/Fev_CSm_m71_1626.chr1.bw\r\n",
      "../tests/data/bigwig/Fev_DR_m70_1623.chr1.bw\r\n",
      "../tests/data/bigwig/Fev_DR_m71_1625.chr1.bw\r\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "ls ../tests/data/bigwig/*chr1.bw"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "To generate junction files from SJ.out.tab, use function [jgem.gtfgffbed.sjtab2sjbed](modules.html#jgem.gtfgffbed.sjtab2sjbed):"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 7,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# sjbed destination\n",
    "si['sjbed_path'] = [os.path.join(BASEDIR, \"SJ/{0}.sj.bed.gz\".format(x)) for x in si['name']]\n",
    "# SJ.out.tab => sjbed\n",
    "from jgem import gtfgffbed as GGB\n",
    "for sjtab, sjbed, acov in si[['sjtab_path','sjbed_path','acov']].values:\n",
    "    scale = 1./acov\n",
    "    GGB.sjtab2sjbed(sjtab,sjbed,scale)"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 8,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",

   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "### SJBED file format\n",
    "\n",
    "As shown above, the tab separated junction file should contain:\n",
    "\n",
    "- **chr**:  chromosome name\n",
    "- **st**: start position\n",
    "- **ed**: end position\n",
    "- **name**: junction name\n",
    "- **ucnt**: unique reads (normalized to average coverage)\n",
    "- **strand**: strand of junction\n",
    "- **mcnt**: non-unique (multimapping) reads (normalized)\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## Assembling individual samples"
   ]
  },

   ]

    "# assemble 4 samples takes about ~10 min \n",
    "from jgem import filenames as FN\n",
    "from jgem import assembler as AS\n",
    "for name,bwfile,sjfile in si[['name','bw_path','sjbed_path']].values:\n",
    "    fn = FN.FileNames(name, bwfile, sjfile, outdir='../tests/out')\n",
    "    p = AS.Assembler(fn,saveintermediates=False)\n",
    "    p.assemble()"
   ]

    "# Evaluate against Gencode.VM4 (~1 min)\n",
    "from jgem import evaluate as EV\n",
    "ens = {} # keep EvalNames objects\n",
    "ems = {} # keep EvalMatch object\n",
    "# Gencode.VM4\n",
    "en_gen4 = EV.EvalNames('../tests/data/assemblies/gencode.vM4.chr1', code='gen4', outdir='../tests/out/')\n",
    "# assign sample code\n",
    "si['scode'] = [x.split('_')[-1].split('.')[0] for x in si['name']]\n",
    "# For each sample\n",
    "for scode, name, bwfile, sjfile in si[['scode','name','bw_path','sjbed_path']].values:\n",
    "    print('process {0}...'.format(name))\n",
    "    sjexbase = '../tests/out/'+name # prefix to .ex.txt.gz and .sj.txt.gz files\n",
    "    assemblycode = 'a'+str(scode) # assembly identifier\n",
    "    datacode = 'd'+str(scode) # data identifier\n",
    "    ens[name] = EV.EvalNames(sjexbase,  code=assemblycode, outdir='../tests/out/') \n",
    "    ems[name] = EV.EvalMatch(en_gen4, ens[name], bwfile, sjfile, datacode=datacode, binsize=100) \n",
    "    ems[name].calculate()"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "INFO outputs are as follows: \n",
    "\n",
    "- detected1: counts of gencode exons/junctions with positive coverage\n",
    "- matched: number of matched exons/junctions \n",
    "- detected2: counts of elements in the assembly \n",
    "- ratio: matched/detected1\n",
    "- ratio2: matched/detected2 \n",
    "\n",
    "These are assesed within different exon classes: \n",
    "\n",
    "- **i**: internal exon (exons bounded by splice junctions)\n",
    "- **5**: 5'exons\n",
    "- **3**: 3'exons\n",
    "- **s**: single exons\n",
    "- **j**: junctions\n",
    "    \n",
    "Classes with **b**, (**5b**,**3b**,**sb**) allow matching to different classes of exons. \n",
    "\n",
    "Matching exons with junction boundary requires the boundaries to match. That is, to match internal exons, they have to be exactly the same (including strand). To match 5'exons, donor site has to the same but the other side does not have to be. To match single exon, they just need to have some overlap. \n",
    "\n",
    "So, we have quite good detection of junctions. About 70% of internal exons are detected. 5',3' exons are worse (< 50%) but if allowed to match to other class of exons, then detection rates get close to the internal exons. Single exon detection rates are bad and about 10%.\n"
   ]
  },

    "# EvalMatch.get_detection_percentages returns a dataframe containing detection percentages \n",
    "dp = PD.DataFrame({n:ems[n].get_detection_percentages().stack() for n in ems})\n",
    "tgt = ['i','5','3','s','j']\n",
    "dp1 = dp.ix[[(x,'%detected 1') for x in tgt]][si['name'].values]\n",
    "dp1.index = tgt\n",
    "ax = dp1.plot(kind='bar', legend=False, figsize=(6,4))\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('detection %')\n",
    "ax.set_xlabel('exons/junctions')\n",
    "ax.legend(loc='center left', bbox_to_anchor=(1,0.5))"

    "These incomplete reconstructions are due to missing junctions or insufficient exon coverages.\n",
    "\n",
    "To evaluate the *completeness* of the reconstruction, we calculate three measures. One is the ratio of gene length. We call this GLC (gene length completenesss). The second measure is the ratio of exon counts (ECC, exon count completeness), and the third is the ratio of junction counts (JCC, junction count completeness).\n",
    "\n",
    "We can visualize these measures by [plot_completeness](modules.html#jgem.evaluate.EvalMatch.plot_completeness) method."

    "## Preparing for merge\n",
    "\n",
    "Since individual cell types express only subsets of the genes, merging assembies is necessary to obtain a more complete picture of the transcriptomes. Moreover, merging should also improve the sensitivity and the completeness of the reconstruction.\n",
    "\n",
    "For merging, we will repeat the assembly process but uses aggregated junctions and coverage bigwigs generated from all exons from all assemblies. We need to prepare these two kinds of files first. For this, we use [MergeInputs class](modules.html#jgem.merge.MergeInputs). \n"
   ]

    "for n in ems2:\n",
    "    dp[n+'_merged'] = ems2[n].get_detection_percentages().stack()\n",
    "tgt = ['i','5','3','s','j']\n",
    "cols = list(si['name'])+[x+'_merged' for x in si['name']]\n",
    "dp1 = dp.ix[[(x,'%detected 1') for x in tgt]][cols]\n",
    "dp1.index = tgt\n",
    "ax = dp1.plot(kind='bar', legend=False, figsize=(10,4))\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('detection %')\n",
    "ax.set_xlabel('exons/junctions')\n",
    "ax.legend(loc='center left', bbox_to_anchor=(1,0.5))"

    "from jgem import annotate as AN\n",
    "g4sjexpre = '../tests/data/assemblies/gencode.vM4.chr1'\n",
    "mergepre = '../tests/out/FevA'\n",

    "cp = AN.Comparator(cref, ctgt, outdir, 'gene_name')\n",
    "cp.annotate(overwrite=False)"

    "Columns are:\n",
    "\n",
    "    cat: exon category (internal, 5',3',single)\n",
    "    gname: assembly gene name\n",
    "    eknown_gen4: exon known against gen4 (k or u)\n",
    "    etcode_gen4: exon code (k.me: known multi-exon, u.se:unknown single exon, etc.)\n",
    "    intergenic_gen4: whether the gene is intergenic \n",
    "    ex_as_ovl_gen4: exon overlaps with gen4 exon in antisense direction\n",
    "    gene_as_ovl_gen4: gene overlaps with gen4 gene in antisense direction\n",
    "    gtcode_gen4: similar to etcode_gen4\n",
    "    gen4_sym0: Gencode.vM4 gene symbol (0 indicates closest one)\n",
